### Most Commonly Tested Topics

**Master these and you're 80% ready:**

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ TOP 20 MUST-KNOW TOPICS                                      │
├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                              │
│ 1.  Service Models (IaaS, PaaS, SaaS) ⭐⭐⭐                  │
│     Know: What each means, examples, shared responsibility   │
│                                                              │
│ 2.  Deployment Models (Public, Private, Hybrid) ⭐⭐⭐        │
│     Know: Differences, when to use each                     │
│                                                              │
│ 3.  Regions & Availability Zones ⭐⭐⭐                       │
│     Know: What they are, why they matter, how they improve   │
│     availability                                             │
│                                                              │
│ 4.  Resource Groups ⭐⭐⭐                                    │
│     Know: Purpose, what happens when you delete one          │
│                                                              │
│ 5.  Subscriptions ⭐⭐⭐                                      │
│     Know: Purpose, why have multiple, billing boundaries     │
│                                                              │
│ 6.  Management Groups ⭐⭐                                    │
│     Know: Purpose, policy inheritance                        │
│                                                              │
│ 7.  Virtual Machines ⭐⭐⭐                                   │
│     Know: IaaS, when to use, availability sets, scale sets   │
│                                                              │
│ 8.  Azure App Service ⭐⭐⭐                                  │
│     Know: PaaS, for web apps, auto-scaling                   │
│                                                              │
│ 9.  Azure Storage ⭐⭐⭐                                      │
│     Know: Blob, File, Queue, Table, redundancy options       │
│                                                              │
│ 10. Azure SQL Database ⭐⭐⭐                                 │
│     Know: PaaS database, automatic backups, scaling          │
│                                                              │
│ 11. Cosmos DB ⭐⭐                                            │
│     Know: Globally distributed, multi-model, NoSQL           │
│                                                              │
│ 12. Virtual Networks ⭐⭐                                     │
│     Know: Isolation, subnets, VPN connections                │
│                                                              │
│ 13. Azure Active Directory ⭐⭐⭐                             │
│     Know: Identity service, SSO, MFA                         │
│                                                              │
│ 14. Azure Monitor ⭐⭐                                        │
│     Know: Metrics, logs, alerts, Log Analytics workspace     │
│                                                              │
│ 15. Azure Advisor ⭐⭐                                        │
│     Know: Recommendations for cost, security, performance    │
│                                                              │
│ 16. Cost Management Tools ⭐⭐⭐                              │
│     Know: Pricing calculator, TCO calculator, Cost Analysis  │
│                                                              │
│ 17. Azure Policy ⭐⭐⭐                                       │
│     Know: Enforce standards, compliance, inheritance         │
│                                                              │
│ 18. RBAC (Role-Based Access Control) ⭐⭐⭐                   │
│     Know: Assign permissions, roles, scope                   │
│                                                              │
│ 19. SLA (Service Level Agreements) ⭐⭐⭐                     │
│     Know: Uptime guarantees, composite SLAs, calculating     │
│                                                              │
│ 20. Support Plans ⭐⭐                                        │
│     Know: Basic, Developer, Standard, Professional Direct    │
│                                                              │
│ Legend: ⭐⭐⭐ = Very likely | ⭐⭐ = Moderately likely         │
│                                                              │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

### Key Facts to Memorize

**Numbers You Need to Know:**

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ MEMORIZE THESE NUMBERS                                       │
│                                                              │
│ SLA PERCENTAGES:                                             │
│ • 99.9%    = ~43 minutes downtime/month                      │
│ • 99.95%   = ~22 minutes downtime/month                      │
│ • 99.99%   = ~4 minutes downtime/month                       │
│ • 99.999%  = ~26 seconds downtime/month                      │
│                                                              │
│ VM AVAILABILITY:                                             │
│ • Single VM (Premium SSD): 99.9%                             │
│ • 2+ VMs in Availability Set: 99.95%                         │
│ • 2+ VMs across Availability Zones: 99.99%                   │
│                                                              │
│ STORAGE REDUNDANCY:                                          │
│ • LRS (Locally Redundant): 3 copies in one datacenter        │
│ • ZRS (Zone Redundant): 3 copies across 3 zones             │
│ • GRS (Geo Redundant): 6 copies (3 local + 3 in pair region)│
│ • RA-GRS: Same as GRS but can READ from secondary           │
│                                                              │
│ FREE TIER LIMITS:                                            │
│ • Azure subscription: $200 credit for 30 days                │
│ • B1S VM: 750 hours/month free for 12 months                 │
│ • Blob storage: 5 GB free for 12 months                      │
│ • SQL Database: 250 GB free for 12 months                    │
│                                                              │
│ REGIONS & ZONES:                                             │
│ • 60+ Azure regions worldwide                                │
│ • 3 availability zones per region (where available)          │
│ • Region pairs for disaster recovery                         │
│                                                              │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

### Test-Taking Strategies

#### During the Exam

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ EXAM DAY TACTICS                                             │
│                                                              │
│ BEFORE YOU START:                                            │
│ □ Read all instructions carefully                           │
│ □ Note which sections allow review                          │
│ □ Use provided whiteboard/notepad for notes                 │
│ □ Take deep breath - you've got this! 💪                    │
│                                                              │
│ TIME MANAGEMENT:                                             │
│ • 60 minutes for 40-60 questions                            │
│ • That's ~1 minute per question                             │
│ • Don't spend more than 2 minutes on any question           │
│ • Flag hard questions, come back if time allows             │
│                                                              │
│ ANSWERING QUESTIONS:                                         │
│ 1. Read question completely before answers                  │
│ 2. Look for key words: "ALWAYS", "NEVER", "MOST", "LEAST"   │
│ 3. Eliminate obviously wrong answers first                  │
│ 4. If stuck between two, go with gut feeling                │
│ 5. Don't overthink - first instinct often correct           │
│                                                              │
│ CASE STUDIES:                                                │
│ • Read scenario once completely                             │
│ • Take notes on key requirements                            │
│ • Answer questions based ONLY on scenario                   │
│ • Don't make assumptions beyond what's stated               │
│                                                              │
│ IF YOU DON'T KNOW AN ANSWER:                                 │
│ • Don't panic!                                              │
│ • Make educated guess                                       │
│ • Never leave blank (no penalty for wrong answers)          │
│ • Use elimination method                                    │
│                                                              │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

### Common Tricky Questions

**Watch out for these question types:**

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ TRICKY QUESTION PATTERNS                                     │
│                                                              │
│ PATTERN 1: "ALWAYS" / "NEVER" Questions                      │
│ ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│ │ Example: "Data in Azure Storage is ALWAYS encrypted"     │ │
│ │                                                          │ │
│ │ Answer: TRUE                                             │ │
│ │ Why: Automatic encryption, can't be disabled             │ │
│ │                                                          │ │
│ │ Tip: If statement says "always" about a security         │ │
│ │ feature in Azure, often TRUE                             │ │
│ └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                              │
│ PATTERN 2: "Which provides the MOST control?"               │
│ ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│ │ Options: IaaS, PaaS, SaaS                                │ │
│ │                                                          │ │
│ │ Answer: IaaS (always)                                    │ │
│ │ Why: Most control = IaaS                                 │ │
│ │      Most convenience = SaaS                             │ │
│ │      Middle ground = PaaS                                │ │
│ └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                              │
│ PATTERN 3: "Best practice to reduce costs?"                 │
│ ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│ │ Look for:                                                │ │
│ │ • Reserved instances                                     │ │
│ │ • Auto-shutdown                                          │ │
│ │ • Right-sizing VMs                                       │ │
│ │ • Deleting unused resources                              │ │
│ │                                                          │ │
│ │ NOT: "Use more VMs" (obviously wrong)                    │ │
│ └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                              │
│ PATTERN 4: "Which allows you to [manage multiple subs]?"    │
│ ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│ │ Options: Resource Groups, Subscriptions, Management      │ │
│ │ Groups                                                   │ │
│ │                                                          │ │
│ │ Answer: Management Groups                                │ │
│ │ Why: Only MGs can contain multiple subscriptions         │ │
│ └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                              │
│ PATTERN 5: "What stores Azure Monitor logs?"                │
│ ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│ │ Common wrong answers:                                    │ │
│ │ • Azure Storage                                          │ │
│ │ • Azure SQL Database                                     │ │
│ │                                                          │ │
│ │ Correct: Log Analytics Workspace                         │ │
│ │ (This specific answer is tested frequently!)             │ │
│ └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                              │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

### Scheduling and Taking the Exam

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ STEP-BY-STEP EXAM PROCESS                                    │
│                                                              │
│ 1. SCHEDULE EXAM                                             │
│    ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│    │ • Go to: learn.microsoft.com/certifications          │ │
│    │ • Find AZ-900 certification                          │ │
│    │ • Click "Schedule exam"                              │ │
│    │ • Choose Pearson VUE                                 │ │
│    │ • Pick date/time/location                            │ │
│    │ • Pay $99 USD                                        │ │
│    │                                                      │ │
│    │ Options:                                             │ │
│    │ A) Test Center (in person, preferred for first time)│ │
│    │ B) Online Proctored (from home, needs webcam)       │ │
│    └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                              │
│ 2. EXAM DAY - TEST CENTER                                    │
│    ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│    │ Before you go:                                       │ │
│    │ • Arrive 15 minutes early                            │ │
│    │ • Bring valid ID (government-issued)                 │ │
│    │ • No phones, bags, notes allowed                     │ │
│    │ • Wear comfortable clothes                           │ │
│    │                                                      │ │
│    │ During exam:                                         │ │
│    │ • You get whiteboard for notes                       │ │
│    │ • 60 minutes for all questions                       │ │
│    │ • No breaks allowed                                  │ │
│    └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                              │
│ 3. EXAM DAY - ONLINE PROCTORED                               │
│    ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│    │ Requirements:                                        │ │
│    │ • Windows or Mac computer                            │ │
│    │ • Webcam + working microphone                        │ │
│    │ • Quiet, private room                                │ │
│    │ • Clear desk (nothing on it!)                        │ │
│    │ • Stable internet connection                         │ │
│    │                                                      │ │
│    │ Check-in process (30 min before):                    │ │
│    │ 1. Install OnVUE software                            │ │
│    │ 2. Take photos of ID                                 │ │
│    │ 3. Take photos of room (360°)                        │ │
│    │ 4. Proctor checks your setup                         │ │
│    │ 5. Exam begins                                       │ │
│    └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                              │
│ 4. AFTER THE EXAM                                            │
│    ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│    │ • Result shown immediately: PASS or FAIL             │ │
│    │ • Score report available online in 24 hours          │ │
│    │ • If PASS: Certificate in 1-2 business days          │ │
│    │ • If FAIL: Can retake after 24 hours                 │ │
│    │ • Must pay again for retake                          │ │
│    └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                              │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### Final Week Checklist

**One week before exam:**

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ FINAL WEEK COUNTDOWN                                         │
│                                                              │
│ 7 DAYS BEFORE:                                               │
│ □ Take full-length practice test                           │
│ □ If score <70%, consider rescheduling                      │
│ □ Make list of weak topics                                  │
│                                                              │
│ 6 DAYS BEFORE:                                               │
│ □ Deep dive into weak topics                                │
│ □ Re-read relevant chapters                                 │
│ □ Watch videos on difficult concepts                        │
│                                                              │
│ 5 DAYS BEFORE:                                               │
│ □ Another practice test                                     │
│ □ Should see improvement                                    │
│ □ Review all wrong answers                                  │
│                                                              │
│ 4 DAYS BEFORE:                                               │
│ □ Memorize key numbers (SLAs, etc.)                         │
│ □ Review flashcards                                         │
│ □ Hands-on practice with Azure portal                      │
│                                                              │
│ 3 DAYS BEFORE:                                               │
│ □ Final practice test                                       │
│ □ Target: 85%+ score                                        │
│ □ Light review of all topics                                │
│                                                              │
│ 2 DAYS BEFORE:                                               │
│ □ Review this chapter's key points                          │
│ □ Go through all flashcards                                 │
│ □ Early night - get good sleep!                             │
│                                                              │
│ 1 DAY BEFORE (Exam eve):                                     │
│ □ Light review only (don't cram!)                           │
│ □ Prepare ID, directions to test center                     │
│ □ Early dinner                                              │
│ □ Relax - watch a movie                                     │
│ □ Sleep early (8+ hours!)                                   │
│                                                              │
│ EXAM DAY MORNING:                                            │
│ □ Good breakfast                                            │
│ □ Quick flashcard review (15 min)                           │
│ □ One practice question set for confidence                  │
│ □ Arrive early / log in early                               │
│ □ Stay calm - you're ready! 💪                              │
│                                                              │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### Emergency Last-Minute Cheat Sheet

**If you only have 24 hours to study:**

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 24-HOUR CRASH COURSE                                         │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 1-2: Service Models                                     │
│ • IaaS = VMs, you manage OS                                 │
│ • PaaS = App Service, Azure manages OS                      │
│ • SaaS = Microsoft 365, just use it                         │
│ • Shared Responsibility Model                               │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 3-4: Azure Core Services                               │
│ • Compute: VMs, App Service, Functions                      │
│ • Storage: Blob, File, Queue, Table                         │
│ • Database: SQL Database, Cosmos DB                         │
│ • Networking: VNet, Load Balancer, VPN                      │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 5-6: Organization                                       │
│ • Resources → Resource Groups → Subscriptions                │
│ • Management Groups for many subs                           │
│ • Azure AD for identity                                     │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 7-8: Regions & Availability                            │
│ • 60+ regions                                               │
│ • 3 availability zones per region                           │
│ • Region pairs for disaster recovery                        │
│ • VM SLAs: 99.9%, 99.95%, 99.99%                            │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 9-10: Security & Identity                              │
│ • Azure AD = Identity service                               │
│ • RBAC = Who can do what                                    │
│ • Azure Policy = What can be created                        │
│ • Defense in depth                                          │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 11-12: Cost Management                                  │
│ • Pricing Calculator = Estimate costs                       │
│ • TCO Calculator = Compare to on-premises                   │
│ • Cost Analysis = Track spending                            │
│ • Budgets and alerts                                        │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 13-14: Monitoring                                       │
│ • Azure Monitor = Metrics and logs                          │
│ • Log Analytics Workspace = Store logs                      │
│ • Azure Advisor = Recommendations                           │
│ • Service Health = Outage info                              │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 15-16: Practice Test 1                                  │
│ • Take full practice exam                                   │
│ • Note all wrong answers                                    │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 17-20: Review Weak Areas                                │
│ • Focus on what you got wrong                               │
│ • Review relevant chapters                                  │
│ • Make quick notes                                          │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 21-22: Practice Test 2                                  │
│ • Should see improvement                                    │
│ • Focus on timing                                           │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 23: Final Review                                        │
│ • Review this cheat sheet                                   │
│ • Go through flashcards                                     │
│ • Memorize SLA numbers                                      │
│                                                              │
│ HOUR 24: REST!                                               │
│ • Stop studying                                             │
│ • Relax and sleep                                           │
│ • Trust your preparation                                    │
│                                                              │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

### 📝 Chapter Summary

**Remember:**

✅ **Exam Basics**
- 40-60 questions, 60 minutes
- $99, immediate pass/fail result
- 700/1000 to pass (~70%)

✅ **Study Smart**
- 4-6 weeks for beginners
- Hands-on practice is essential
- Practice tests in final week
- Don't cram night before

✅ **Top Topics to Master**
- Service models (IaaS/PaaS/SaaS)
- Shared Responsibility Model
- Azure core services
- Resource organization
- Cost management

✅ **Test Day**
- Read questions completely
- Manage your time
- Don't leave blanks
- Stay calm and confident

---

### 🎯 Final Practice Questions

**Question 1:**
You need the MOST control over operating system. Which service model?

A) SaaS  
B) PaaS  
C) IaaS  
D) All provide same control

**Question 2:**
What stores Azure Monitor logs?

A) Azure Storage Account  
B) Log Analytics Workspace  
C) Azure SQL Database  
D) Resource Group

**Question 3:**
Single VM with Premium SSD has what SLA?

A) 99.9%  
B) 99.95%  
C) 99.99%  
D) No SLA

**Question 4:**
Which lets you manage multiple subscriptions?

A) Resource Groups  
B) Management Groups  
C) Azure Policy  
D) RBAC

**Question 5:**
Data in Azure Storage is ALWAYS encrypted?

A) True  
B) False

---

### ✍️ Answers

**1: C** - IaaS gives most control (you manage OS)  
**2: B** - Log Analytics Workspace (not Storage!)  
**3: A** - 99.9% (single VM with Premium SSD)  
**4: B** - Management Groups contain subscriptions  
**5: A** - True (automatic, can't disable)

---
